<userid>100622545416937587727</userid>< review>
Not a good experience. I tried to go there on 2 days. First day, they did not mention I can take car to the entrance. I kept my car in uphill near to the road and then hiked down. Elevation is steep and not for occasional hiker. Entrance is 1 mile down from the uphill and beach is another 1 mile. When I reach entrance, I saw many cars going in even though uphill it is mentioned as parking full. Hike is steeper from entrance to the beach. People can't take lift as there is a fine to that. Not very helpful to people who can't hike back or are having trouble. On Second day I went with my car. Ignored the parking full board on uphill like others and went till the entrance. The car before me was allowed but they stopped me citing parking full and asked me to return. I said I can wait there and when slot opens up I will go but for that I have to wait uphill and try in an hour. I could have done that but meanwhile they could have let anyone in. They also don't have counter or check on how many are in or coming out. One car was returning when I was talking to them but they said that does not guarantee that a space opens up. Not sure where else one would park their cars if not in parking space. All in all, it is not arranged properly. Rangers are not helpful in this regards. Don't have good rules or process around vehicle traffic. Also there is no signage on distance for hiker. For wilderness it is all good but for a well managed and popular state park, it seems horrendous.< /review>

< rating>

< Text>
First time at D.L. Bliss SP- 4th July 2020-
Stayed at East Ridge Campground a 10 min walk down to Lester Beach.
2 pm check-in. Very maintained and safe saw camp rangers do their rounds every couple hours. HELPFUL INFO: Has many bathrooms some with showers. Only 3 bathrooms have a token machines if you want to shower. $1= 1 token = 3 minutes. Water gets lukewarm, and you have flushing toilets. Firewood for purchase is $10 a bundle (includes 4 logs).
E. Ridge campgrounds were super spacious easily fit 4 tents- include locker, fire pit, picnic table and grill. Campgrounds have enough room for 2 cars. Price of 1 is covered with reservation the second has a $10 fee every night. Lester beach is beautiful but WARNING: no joke @ 830 am more then 3/4 of the parking spots were taken. By 1030 am they had already CLOSED/FULL the parking area. There's maybe 50 spots and the park opens at 730 am.< /Text>

<review>A beautiful state park with an adorable visitor center/gift shop. The educational displays of the local wildlife (lots of taxidermy) is fantastic & makes for some great teachable moments. We were the only people there except for the ranger/clerk who was knowledgeable, friendly & very helpful. This was my first trip to the Lake Tahoe area & it's a photographer's dream. < review>
Beautiful spot with great trails, 4 stars for the busyness. I don't usually mind people on the trails (nature is for everyone!), but emerald bay on a nice day is full of boats full of drunk 20 something's blasting tunes and screaming as they take turns jumping in the icy water. For beauty this place is 5 stars, for overall ambiance I'd give it 3.5, so we'll settle on 4! Did a run on rubicon trail so really saw the whole area.

A decent spot to hunt porcinis too if you know what you're looking for!<//review>

< Review>
I‚Äôll begin by saying this place is utterly gorgeous. However my friends and I had quiet the negative experience here. First and foremost, you‚Äôre allowed to bring your dog, but they are required to be leashed 24/7 and you‚Äôre not allowed to take them on any trails or down to the water. My dog was basically not allowed to do anything but stay tied to a tree. Absurd.
Secondly, the yellow jackets are insane out there. Cooking is nearly impossible with them around. We made breakfast and had to fight off like 50 yellow jackets. It‚Äôs horrible.
Lastly, the park rangers and state troopers are unbearable. We were harassed multiple times by the state troopers and park rangers. We went down to the lake for a couple hours and came back to a ledger of items they removed from our camp. Yes we accidentally left a ice chest out that had some hummus and various things. But they went through all our belongings and took things like our ipbrofen, my weed and pipe, and a whole list of things that apparently bears look for. I understand the food issue because bears are very active in this area but our privacy was fully invaded. The following day we had 2 state troopers come to our camp and tell us we had 30 minutes to pack our things and leave the camp or they were going to arrest us. They showed up with their hands on their gun holsters and quiet literally treated us like criminals. We had 1 more day of camp paid for ($45/night) and they would not refund us. We were kicked out because me and 2 friends were up late laughing and playing cards. Apparently that‚Äôs grounds for being kicked out of this camp area. My friend and I are from Oregon and have never experienced such a hostile camping environment. We were forced to leave and find a hotel in town. Again, beautiful camping area, but I would never go camp their again.<//Review>

<time>1467838038869<//time><rating>1< /rating>< review>
DO NOT MOVE HERE

I haven't even moved in yet. I put the $100 deposit on an apartment that opens in August 1 month ago and  I am already incredibly unsatisfied and out of $100.

1. When I filled out the application for the apartment and put my $100 deposit I made it clear that I was going to continue to look for another place because I wanted to move in sooner than August. I specifically asked if I would be refunded my $100 if I did find another home. I was told the only thing non-refundable is the $35 credit check.

2. No one disclosed any of the criminal activity that has recently happened at Emerald Pointe to me. Modesto Police Department confirmed that in the last 4 weeks there has be 2 gang related assults, 2 car thefts, and 1 burgulary. How can you feel good about renting to a single mom and her 2 kids and not feel that it is necassary to disclose this kind of information - especially violent crimes.

3. When I called and asked about getting my $100 refunded, the property manager got rude and told me that because my application was already approved she didn't HAVE to give the $100 back - making it sound like she could, but wasn't going to. When I asked if I could talk to her manager she told me she was the manager. When I asked for the information regarding who owns Emerald Pointe she told me she would not disclose that information. WORST COSTUMER SERVICE.

I'm out $100, but at least myself or my family wasn't caught in the crossfire of any criminal activity. You can tell by looking at these apartments that they don't have much to offer - they intice you with the two pools, basketball court, and play ground that you probably wouldn't be safe using. I tried to give them some credit for being under new management but was quickly proven wrong in doing so - these apartments are still the dump everyone says they are. I'm just relieved I found this out prior to moving in.</review>

< Text>
Just goes to show you.. you should read reviews before doing business with anyone these days!  It seems that I have fallen victim to the super secret, (made up) return/exchange policy at 5.11 as well? A few days ago I bought 3 pair of pants as well as various other items.  The next day, I pulled the tags off and was going to put a pair of pants on.  It was then that I realized that they were a bit bigger in the waist than I realized in the store.  So I put the tags in the pocket and took them back to the store with the receipt.  I just wanted to exchange for a smaller size, then make an additional purchase that would have amounted to about $1000.00.  2 pairs of 300.00 boots and a half dozen shirts.  The sales person (who was my original salesperson days before)   Explained to me that if the tags have been removed, the store policy was no refunds / no exchanges. I pointed out on my receipt that is not the policy stated in writing?  He said no... it's not in writing it's just a store policy? Then  I begin to argue with him and explained that that's the most ridiculous thing I've ever heard of in my life, we go back-and-forth.  Then he changes his mind about the unwritten policy and he says to me "would you settle for two out of three? I said two out of three what? He said well I can let you exchange two pairs but the third pair has been washed and we can't exchange those. I said to him that they never went more than 3 feet from the bag they've not been washed and they were exactly in the condition which I bought them.  He argued back-and-forth with me again and told me I could call customer service. So I called customer service while standing in the store the phone rang and rang finally somebody answered I explained the problem.. they put me on hold for several minutes came back and said that there was nobody there that could help me and there's nothing they could do for me at that time? What?  So much for customer service I guess? They suggested that I talk to the store manager.   So I hung up the phone and asked the salesperson who is the store manager?    He replied Kristy.   I said fine when would she be back in the store so that I could talk to her about this transaction? I swear I am not making this up...the sales guy said that he's not allowed to tell customers when the manager is going to be in the store it's against store policy. I swear to God I thought I was on an episode of the twilight zone! I said so what do I do?  Do I just call every 20 minutes day after day until she answers the phone to figure out when she's there?  He just said I guess so?  What the???  I will say it's a pretty cool store and they have some pretty cool items.    I am just completely baffled by the way they do business. So, in the end, I asked for a complete refund on the two pairs of pants he didn't argue about, and I told him I would just throw the third pair in the trash and that I would never be back,  I don't think he really cared?   Needless to say, they didn't get it the other thousand dollar sale for me tonight night either?   Way too much work to do business with these guys... it feels like they just make it up as they go? They are great when taking your money... but God help you if you need a little service after the sale.  Ridiculous.  Buyers beware!!!

Just remembered this as well...  while I was in the store for the original purchase, the salesperson told me that the sizes can vary for any two pairs of the same pants.  I was told that it was due to the fact that they are made in two different factories in China.. and they have very little control over the output?  You can tell because the labels inside the pants are different?  The pants are $69.00?  Maybe for that price they should make them in the USA?  Just a thought.< /Text>

<user_name>Alyssamarie Smith</user_name>< Pictures>
None</Pictures>
< text>
5.11 Store. Ah. The store for military, law enforcement, fire, EMS, and people that like to spend $70+ to dress up and look like they're doing something tactical. Haha. All jokes aside, I'm extremely glad that they have an actual 5.11 store in Sacramento. My go to 5.11 establishment before didn't have a wide variety of womens apparel, but lo and behold when this baby opened up I was in heaven!! They have about 5-6 different womens pants with all of the sizes, polos, gun range gear, belts, shirts, tanks, you name it! They do not skimp on ladies products.

Oh... and for the guys, they have pretty much have all the supplies off the website for you. Hats, patches, pants, polos, etc...

They also have write in the rain supplies, knives, ANSI certified sunglasses, med bag gear stuff, molle gear stuff, belts, shoes and hydroflasks.

Anyway, if you love tactical stuff. You'll be in heaven. Go here, you won't regret it. Also if you love a good sale, go all the way in the back by the shoes. Sometimes they have it up in the front by the women's gear. You're welcome. :)< /text>
